edX Support

For questions on course lectures, homework, tools, or materials for this course, post in the course discussion forum.

Have general questions about edX? You can find lots of helpful information in the edX FAQ.

Have a question about something specific? You can contact the edX general support team directly:



Please note: The edX support team is English speaking. While we will do our best to address your inquiry in any language, our responses will be in English.

Describe what you were doing when you encountered the issue. Include any details that will help us to troubleshoot, including error messages that you saw.

Thank You!

Thank you for your inquiry or feedback. We typically respond to a request within one business day, Monday to Friday. In the meantime, please review our detailed FAQs where most questions have already been answered.

Course Week 3: Structured Types Problem Set 3 Problem 4
<div class="xblock xblock-student_view xblock-student_view-vertical" data-runtime-class="LmsRuntime" data-init="VerticalStudentView" data-course-id="course-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017" data-request-token="5db767ff51db11e79f4b0e12f2404950" data-runtime-version="1" data-usage-id="block-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017+type@vertical+block@c949e378fb2d42f1b30877fc01b3ef5b" data-block-type="vertical"> <h2 class="hd hd-2 unit-title">Introduction</h2> <div class="bookmark-button-wrapper"> <button class="btn btn-link bookmark-button " aria-pressed="false" data-bookmark-id="PasteurTran,block-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017+type@vertical+block@c949e378fb2d42f1b30877fc01b3ef5b" data-bookmarks-api-url="/api/bookmarks/v1/bookmarks/"> <span class="bookmark-text">Bookmark this page</span> </button> </div> <div class="vert-mod"> <div class="vert vert-0" data-id="block-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017+type@html+block@5e117d71433647eaa6de63434641c011"> <div class="xblock xblock-student_view xblock-student_view-html xmodule_display xmodule_HtmlModule" data-runtime-class="LmsRuntime" data-init="XBlockToXModuleShim" data-block-type="html" data-request-token="5db767ff51db11e79f4b0e12f2404950" data-runtime-version="1" data-usage-id="block-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017+type@html+block@5e117d71433647eaa6de63434641c011" data-type="HTMLModule" data-course-id="course-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017"> <script type="json/xblock-args" class="xblock-json-init-args"> {"xmodule-type": "HTMLModule"} </script> <div id="edx-notes-wrapper-214434759058732526599542864194310427205" class="edx-notes-wrapper"> <div class="edx-notes-wrapper-content"><p>Note: Do not be intimidated by this problem! It's actually easier than it looks. We will 'scaffold' this problem, guiding you through the creation of helper functions before you implement the actual game.</p> <p>For this problem, you will implement a variation of the classic wordgame Hangman. For those of you who are unfamiliar with the rules, you may read all about it <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hangman%20%28game%29" target="_blank">here</a>. In this problem, the second player will always be the computer, who will be picking a word at random.</p> <p>In this problem, you will implement a <b>function</b>, called <code>hangman</code>, that will start up and carry out an interactive Hangman game between a player and the computer. Before we get to this function, we'll first implement a few helper functions to get you going.</p> <p>For this problem, you will need the code files <code><a href="//d37djvu3ytnwxt.cloudfront.net/assets/courseware/v1/2dc6d29d0b7e8620e53d286dd9213a88/asset-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017+type@asset+block/ps3_hangman.py">ps3_hangman.py</a></code> and <code><a href="//d37djvu3ytnwxt.cloudfront.net/assets/courseware/v1/b537aed0f6d1e3c4a25fa1e640533c85/asset-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017+type@asset+block/words.txt">words.txt</a>.</code>&nbsp;Right-click on each and hit "Save Link As". <strong>Be sure to save them in same directory.</strong> Open and run the file <code>ps3_hangman.py</code> without making any modifications to it, in order to ensure that everything is set up correctly. By "open and run" we mean do the following:</p> <ul> <li>Go to your IDE. From the File menu, choose "Open".</li> <li>Find the file <code>ps3_hangman.py</code> and choose it.</li> <li>The template <code>ps3_hangman.py</code> file should now be open.&nbsp;Run the file.</li> </ul> <p>The code we have given you loads in a list of words from a file. If everything is working okay, after a small delay, you should see the following printed out:</p> <pre><code> Loading word list from file... 55909 words loaded. </code></pre> <p>If you see an <code>IOError</code> instead (e.g., "No such file or directory"), you should change the value of the <code>WORDLIST_FILENAME</code> constant (defined near the top of the file) to the <b>complete</b> pathname for the file <code>words.txt</code> (This will vary based on where you saved the file). Windows users, change the backslashes to forward slashes, like below.</p> <p>For example, if you saved <code>ps3_hangman.py</code> and <code>words.txt</code> in the directory "C:/Users/Ana/" change the line:&nbsp;</p> <p><code style="background-color: #ffffff; font-size: 16px;">WORDLIST_FILENAME = "words.txt"</code>&nbsp; to something like</p> <p><code style="font-size: 1em; line-height: 1.6em; background-color: #ffffff;">WORDLIST_FILENAME = "C:/Users/Ana/words.txt"</code></p> <p><b style="font-size: 1em; line-height: 1.6em;">This folder will vary depending on where you saved the files.</b></p> <p>The file <code>ps3_hangman.py</code> has a number of already implemented functions you can use while writing up your solution. You can ignore the code between the following comments, though you should read and understand how to use each helper function by reading the docstrings:</p> <pre><code> # ----------------------------------- # Helper code # You don't need to understand this helper code, # but you will have to know how to use the functions # (so be sure to read the docstrings!) . . . # (end of helper code) # ----------------------------------- </code></pre> <p>You will want to do all of your coding for this problem within this file as well because you will be writing a program that depends on each function you write.</p> <h4>Requirements</h4> <p>Here are the requirements for your game:</p> <ol> <li> <p>The computer must select a word at random from the list of available words that was provided in <code>words.txt</code>. The functions for loading the word list and selecting a random word have already been provided for you in <code>ps3_hangman.py</code>.</p> </li> <li> <p>The game must be interactive; the flow of the game should go as follows:</p> <ul> <li> <p>At the start of the game, let the user know how many letters the computer's word contains.</p> </li> <li> <p>Ask the user to supply one guess (i.e. letter) per round.</p> </li> <li> <p>The user should receive feedback immediately after each guess about whether their guess appears in the computer's word.</p> </li> <li> <p>After each round, you should also display to the user the partially guessed word so far, as well as letters that the user has not yet guessed.</p> </li> </ul> </li> <li>Some additional rules of the game: <ul> <li> <p>A user is allowed 8 guesses. Make sure to remind the user of how many guesses s/he has left after each round. Assume that players will only ever submit one character at a time (A-Z).</p> </li> <li> <p>A user loses a guess <b>only</b> when s/he guesses incorrectly.</p> </li> <li> <p>If the user guesses the same letter twice, do not take away a guess - instead, print a message letting them know they've already guessed that letter and ask them to try again.</p> </li> <li> <p>The game should end when the user constructs the full word or runs out of guesses. If the player runs out of guesses (s/he "loses"), reveal the word to the user when the game ends.</p> </li> </ul> </li> </ol> <section class="hints"> <h3>Sample Output</h3> <div class="collapsible"><header><a id="ht1l" href="#">The output of a winning game should look like this...</a></header> <section id="ht1"> <pre><code> Loading word list from file... 55900 words loaded. Welcome to the game, Hangman! I am thinking of a word that is 4 letters long. ------------- You have 8 guesses left. Available letters: abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: a Good guess: _ a_ _ ------------ You have 8 guesses left. Available letters: bcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: a Oops! You've already guessed that letter: _ a_ _ ------------ You have 8 guesses left. Available letters: bcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: s Oops! That letter is not in my word: _ a_ _ ------------ You have 7 guesses left. Available letters: bcdefghijklmnopqrtuvwxyz Please guess a letter: t Good guess: ta_ t ------------ You have 7 guesses left. Available letters: bcdefghijklmnopqruvwxyz Please guess a letter: r Oops! That letter is not in my word: ta_ t ------------ You have 6 guesses left. Available letters: bcdefghijklmnopquvwxyz Please guess a letter: m Oops! That letter is not in my word: ta_ t ------------ You have 5 guesses left. Available letters: bcdefghijklnopquvwxyz Please guess a letter: c Good guess: tact ------------ Congratulations, you won! </code></pre> </section> </div> <div class="collapsible"><header><a id="ht2l" href="#">And the output of a losing game should look like this...</a></header> <section id="ht2"> <pre><code> Loading word list from file... 55900 words loaded. Welcome to the game Hangman! I am thinking of a word that is 4 letters long ----------- You have 8 guesses left Available Letters: abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: a Oops! That letter is not in my word: _ _ _ _ ----------- You have 7 guesses left Available Letters: bcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: b Oops! That letter is not in my word: _ _ _ _ ----------- You have 6 guesses left Available Letters: cdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: c Oops! That letter is not in my word: _ _ _ _ ----------- You have 5 guesses left Available Letters: defghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: d Oops! That letter is not in my word: _ _ _ _ ----------- You have 4 guesses left Available Letters: efghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: e Good guess: e_ _ e ----------- You have 4 guesses left Available Letters: fghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: f Oops! That letter is not in my word: e_ _ e ----------- You have 3 guesses left Available Letters: ghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: g Oops! That letter is not in my word: e_ _ e ----------- You have 2 guesses left Available Letters: hijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: h Oops! That letter is not in my word: e_ _ e ----------- You have 1 guesses left Available Letters: ijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: i Oops! That letter is not in my word: e_ _ e ----------- Sorry, you ran out of guesses. The word was else. </code></pre> </section> </div> </section> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>On the next page, we'll break down the problem into logical subtasks, creating helper functions you will need to have in order for this game to work.</p></div> </div> <script type="text/javascript"> (function (require) { Please translate the word 'comments'. fmt = gettext('%(comments_count)s %(span_sr_open)scomments %(span_close)s'); } print(interpolate(fmt, data, true)); %> </span> </div> </a> </li> </script> <script aria-hidden="true" type="text/template" id="search-alert-template"> <div class="search-alert <%- css_class %>" id="search-alert-<%- cid %>"> <div class="search-alert-content"> <p class="message"><%= HtmlUtils.ensureHtml(messageHtml) %></p> </div> <div class="search-alert-controls"> <button class="btn-link dismiss control control-dismiss" title="<%- gettext('Close') %>"> <span class="icon fa fa-remove" aria-hidden="true"></span> </button> </div> </div> </script> <script aria-hidden="true" type="text/template" id="new-post-template"> <form class="forum-new-post-form"> <h<%- startHeader %> class="thread-title"><%- gettext("Add a Post") %></h<%- startHeader %>> <% if (mode === 'inline') { %> <button class="btn-default add-post-cancel"> <span class="sr"><%- gettext('Cancel') %></span> <span class="fa fa-close" aria-hidden="true"></span> </button> <% } %> <ul class="post-errors" style="display: none"></ul> <div class="forum-new-post-form-wrapper"></div> <% if (group_options) { %> <div class="post-field group-selector-wrapper <% if (!is_commentable_divided) { print('disabled'); &lt;/h3&gt; &lt;div class=&#34;problem-progress&#34; id=&#34;block-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017+type@problem+block@addd0db3b3284610944ac1bf59ba60db-problem-progress&#34;&gt;&lt;/div&gt; &lt;div class=&#34;problem&#34;&gt; &lt;div&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;p&gt; Next, implement the function &lt;code&gt;getGuessedWord&lt;/code&gt; that takes in two parameters - a string, &lt;code&gt;secretWord&lt;/code&gt;, and a list of letters, &lt;code&gt;lettersGuessed&lt;/code&gt;. This function returns a string that is comprised of letters and underscores, based on what letters in &lt;code&gt;lettersGuessed&lt;/code&gt; are in &lt;code&gt;secretWord&lt;/code&gt;. This shouldn&#39;t be too different from &lt;code&gt;isWordGuessed&lt;/code&gt;!&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Example Usage:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;pre&gt;&amp;gt;&amp;gt;&amp;gt; secretWord = &#39;apple&#39; &amp;gt;&amp;gt;&amp;gt; lettersGuessed = [&#39;e&#39;, &#39;i&#39;, &#39;k&#39;, &#39;p&#39;, &#39;r&#39;, &#39;s&#39;] &amp;gt;&amp;gt;&amp;gt; print(getGuessedWord(secretWord, lettersGuessed)) &#39;_ pp_ e&#39;&lt;/pre&gt;&lt;p&gt;When inserting underscores into your string, it&#39;s a good idea to add at least a space after each one, so it&#39;s clear to the user how many unguessed letters are left in the string (compare the readability of &lt;code&gt;____&lt;/code&gt; with &lt;code&gt;_ _ _ _ &lt;/code&gt;). This is called &lt;i&gt;usability&lt;/i&gt; - it&#39;s very important, when programming, to consider the usability of your program. If users find your program difficult to understand or operate, they won&#39;t use it!&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;For this problem, you are free to use spacing in any way you wish - our grader will only check that the letters and underscores are in the proper order; it will not look at spacing. We do encourage you to think about usability when designing. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;For this function, you may assume that all the letters in &lt;code&gt;secretWord&lt;/code&gt; and &lt;code&gt;lettersGuessed&lt;/code&gt; are lowercase.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div class=&#34;wrapper-problem-response&#34; tabindex=&#34;-1&#34; aria-label=&#34;Question 1&#34; role=&#34;group&#34;&gt;&lt;div id=&#34;textbox_addd0db3b3284610944ac1bf59ba60db_2_1&#34; class=&#34;capa_inputtype textbox cminput&#34;&gt;&lt;label class=&#34;sr problem-group-label&#34; for=&#34;cm-textarea-addd0db3b3284610944ac1bf59ba60db_2_1&#34;&gt;Code Editor&lt;/label&gt;&lt;textarea rows=&#34;30&#34; cols=&#34;70&#34; name=&#34;input_addd0db3b3284610944ac1bf59ba60db_2_1&#34; aria-label=&#34;python editor&#34; aria-describedby=&#34;answer_addd0db3b3284610944ac1bf59ba60db_2_1&#34; id=&#34;input_addd0db3b3284610944ac1bf59ba60db_2_1&#34; tabindex=&#34;0&#34; data-mode=&#34;python&#34; data-tabsize=&#34;4&#34; data-linenums=&#34;true&#34;&gt; def getGuessedWord(secretWord, lettersGuessed): &#39;&#39;&#39; secretWord: string, the word the user is guessing lettersGuessed: list, what letters have been guessed so far returns: string, comprised of letters and underscores that represents what letters in secretWord have been guessed so far. &#39;&#39;&#39; Please translate the word 'comments'. fmt = gettext('%(comments_count)s %(span_sr_open)scomments %(span_close)s'); } print(interpolate(fmt, data, true)); %> </span> </div> </a> </li> </script> <script aria-hidden="true" type="text/template" id="search-alert-template"> <div class="search-alert <%- css_class %>" id="search-alert-<%- cid %>"> <div class="search-alert-content"> <p class="message"><%= HtmlUtils.ensureHtml(messageHtml) %></p> </div> <div class="search-alert-controls"> <button class="btn-link dismiss control control-dismiss" title="<%- gettext('Close') %>"> <span class="icon fa fa-remove" aria-hidden="true"></span> </button> </div> </div> </script> <script aria-hidden="true" type="text/template" id="new-post-template"> <form class="forum-new-post-form"> <h<%- startHeader %> class="thread-title"><%- gettext("Add a Post") %></h<%- startHeader %>> <% if (mode === 'inline') { %> <button class="btn-default add-post-cancel"> <span class="sr"><%- gettext('Cancel') %></span> <span class="fa fa-close" aria-hidden="true"></span> </button> <% } %> <ul class="post-errors" style="display: none"></ul> <div class="forum-new-post-form-wrapper"></div> <% if (group_options) { %> <div class="post-field group-selector-wrapper <% if (!is_commentable_divided) { print('disabled'); data-bookmark-id="PasteurTran,block-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017+type@vertical+block@7f38cc168844466ba3d3fdefb420f3ca" data-bookmarks-api-url="/api/bookmarks/v1/bookmarks/"> <span data-id="block-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017+type@problem+block@7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457"> <div class="xblock xblock-student_view xblock-student_view-problem xmodule_display xmodule_CapaModule" data-runtime-class="LmsRuntime" data-init="XBlockToXModuleShim" data-block-type="problem" data-request-token="5db767ff51db11e79f4b0e12f2404950" data-runtime-version="1" data-usage-id="block-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017+type@problem+block@7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457" data-type="Problem" data-course-id="course-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017"> <script type="json/xblock-args" class="xblock-json-init-args"> {"xmodule-type": "Problem"} </script> <div id="problem_7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457" class="problems-wrapper" role="group" aria-labelledby="7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457-problem-title" data-problem-id="block-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017+type@problem+block@7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457" data-url="/courses/course-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017/xblock/block-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017+type@problem+block@7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457/handler/xmodule_handler" data-problem-score="0.0" data-problem-total-possible="15.0" data-attempts-used="0" data-content=" &lt;h3 class=&#34;hd hd-3 problem-header&#34; id=&#34;7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457-problem-title&#34; aria-describedby=&#34;block-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017+type@problem+block@7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457-problem-progress&#34; tabindex=&#34;-1&#34;&gt; Problem 4 - The Game &lt;/h3&gt; &lt;div class=&#34;problem-progress&#34; id=&#34;block-v1:MITx+6.00.1x+2T2017+type@problem+block@7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457-problem-progress&#34;&gt;&lt;/div&gt; &lt;div class=&#34;problem&#34;&gt; &lt;div&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Now you will implement the function &lt;code&gt;hangman&lt;/code&gt;, which takes one parameter - the &lt;code&gt;secretWord&lt;/code&gt; the user is to guess. This starts up an interactive game of Hangman between the user and the computer. Be sure you take advantage of the three helper functions, &lt;code&gt;isWordGuessed&lt;/code&gt;, &lt;code&gt;getGuessedWord&lt;/code&gt;, and &lt;code&gt;getAvailableLetters&lt;/code&gt;, that you&#39;ve defined in the previous part.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;h4&gt;Hints:&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;You should start by noticing where we&#39;re using the provided functions (at the top of &lt;code&gt;ps3_hangman.py&lt;/code&gt;) to load the words and pick a random one. Note that the functions &lt;code&gt;loadWords&lt;/code&gt; and &lt;code&gt;chooseWord&lt;/code&gt; should only be used on your local machine, not in the tutor. When you enter in your solution in the tutor, you only need to give your &lt;code&gt;hangman&lt;/code&gt; function.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;Consider using &lt;code&gt;lower()&lt;/code&gt; to convert user input to lower case. For example:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;pre&gt;guess = &#39;A&#39; guessInLowerCase = guess.lower()&lt;/pre&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;Consider writing additional helper functions if you need them!&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;p&gt;There are four important pieces of information you may wish to store:&lt;/p&gt;&lt;ol&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;code&gt;secretWord&lt;/code&gt;: The word to guess.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;code&gt;lettersGuessed&lt;/code&gt;: The letters that have been guessed so far.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;code&gt;mistakesMade&lt;/code&gt;: The number of incorrect guesses made so far.&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;code&gt;availableLetters&lt;/code&gt;: The letters that may still be guessed. Every time a player guesses a letter, the guessed letter must be removed from &lt;code&gt;availableLetters&lt;/code&gt; (and if they guess a letter that is not in &lt;code&gt;availableLetters&lt;/code&gt;, you should print a message telling them they&#39;ve already guessed that - so try again!).&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;section class=&#34;hints&#34;&gt;&lt;h3&gt;Sample Output&lt;/h3&gt;&lt;div class=&#34;collapsible&#34;&gt;&lt;header&gt;&lt;a href=&#34;#&#34; id=&#34;ht1l&#34;&gt;The output of a winning game should look like this...&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/header&gt;&lt;section id=&#34;ht1&#34;&gt;&lt;pre&gt; Loading word list from file... 55900 words loaded. Welcome to the game, Hangman! I am thinking of a word that is 4 letters long. ------------- You have 8 guesses left. Available letters: abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: a Good guess: _ a_ _ ------------ You have 8 guesses left. Available letters: bcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: a Oops! You&#39;ve already guessed that letter: _ a_ _ ------------ You have 8 guesses left. Available letters: bcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: s Oops! That letter is not in my word: _ a_ _ ------------ You have 7 guesses left. Available letters: bcdefghijklmnopqrtuvwxyz Please guess a letter: t Good guess: ta_ t ------------ You have 7 guesses left. Available letters: bcdefghijklmnopqruvwxyz Please guess a letter: r Oops! That letter is not in my word: ta_ t ------------ You have 6 guesses left. Available letters: bcdefghijklmnopquvwxyz Please guess a letter: m Oops! That letter is not in my word: ta_ t ------------ You have 5 guesses left. Available letters: bcdefghijklnopquvwxyz Please guess a letter: c Good guess: tact ------------ Congratulations, you won! &lt;/pre&gt;&lt;/section&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&#34;collapsible&#34;&gt;&lt;header&gt;&lt;a href=&#34;#&#34; id=&#34;ht2l&#34;&gt;And the output of a losing game should look like this...&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/header&gt;&lt;section id=&#34;ht2&#34;&gt;&lt;pre&gt; Loading word list from file... 55900 words loaded. Welcome to the game Hangman! I am thinking of a word that is 4 letters long. ----------- You have 8 guesses left. Available Letters: abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: a Oops! That letter is not in my word: _ _ _ _ ----------- You have 7 guesses left. Available Letters: bcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: b Oops! That letter is not in my word: _ _ _ _ ----------- You have 6 guesses left. Available Letters: cdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: c Oops! That letter is not in my word: _ _ _ _ ----------- You have 5 guesses left. Available Letters: defghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: d Oops! That letter is not in my word: _ _ _ _ ----------- You have 4 guesses left. Available Letters: efghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: e Good guess: e_ _ e ----------- You have 4 guesses left. Available Letters: fghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: f Oops! That letter is not in my word: e_ _ e ----------- You have 3 guesses left. Available Letters: ghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: g Oops! That letter is not in my word: e_ _ e ----------- You have 2 guesses left. Available Letters: hijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: h Oops! That letter is not in my word: e_ _ e ----------- You have 1 guesses left. Available Letters: ijklmnopqrstuvwxyz Please guess a letter: i Oops! That letter is not in my word: e_ _ e ----------- Sorry, you ran out of guesses. The word was else. &lt;/pre&gt;&lt;/section&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/section&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;p&gt;Note that if you choose to use the helper functions &lt;code&gt;isWordGuessed&lt;/code&gt;, &lt;code&gt;getGuessedWord&lt;/code&gt;, or &lt;code&gt;getAvailableLetters&lt;/code&gt;, you do not need to paste your definitions in the box. We have supplied our implementations of these functions for your use in this part of the problem. If you use additional helper functions, you will need to paste those definitions here. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Your function should include calls to &lt;code&gt;input&lt;/code&gt; to get the user&#39;s guess. &lt;/p&gt;&lt;section class=&#34;hints&#34;&gt;&lt;div class=&#34;collapsible&#34;&gt;&lt;header&gt;&lt;a href=&#34;#&#34; id=&#34;id71&#34;&gt;Why does my Output Have &lt;code&gt;None&lt;/code&gt; at Various Places?&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/header&gt;&lt;section id=&#34;id71&#34;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;code&gt;None&lt;/code&gt; is a keyword and it comes from the fact that you are printing the result of a function that does not return anything. For example: &lt;pre&gt; def foo(x): print(x) &lt;/pre&gt; If you just call the function with &lt;code&gt;foo(3)&lt;/code&gt;, you will see output: &lt;pre&gt; 3 #-- because the function printed the variable &lt;/pre&gt; However, if you do &lt;code&gt;print(foo(3))&lt;/code&gt;, you will see output: &lt;pre&gt; 3 #-- because the function printed the variable None #-- because you printed the function (and hence the return) &lt;/pre&gt; All functions return something. If a function you write does not return anything (and just prints something to the console), then the default action in Python is to &lt;code&gt;return None&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/section&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/section&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div class=&#34;wrapper-problem-response&#34; tabindex=&#34;-1&#34; aria-label=&#34;Question 1&#34; role=&#34;group&#34;&gt;&lt;div id=&#34;textbox_7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457_2_1&#34; class=&#34;capa_inputtype textbox cminput&#34;&gt;&lt;label class=&#34;sr problem-group-label&#34; for=&#34;cm-textarea-7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457_2_1&#34;&gt;Code Editor&lt;/label&gt;&lt;textarea rows=&#34;40&#34; cols=&#34;70&#34; name=&#34;input_7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457_2_1&#34; aria-label=&#34;python editor&#34; aria-describedby=&#34;answer_7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457_2_1&#34; id=&#34;input_7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457_2_1&#34; tabindex=&#34;0&#34; data-mode=&#34;python&#34; data-tabsize=&#34;4&#34; data-linenums=&#34;true&#34;&gt; def hangman(secretWord): &#39;&#39;&#39; secretWord: string, the secret word to guess. Starts up an interactive game of Hangman. * At the start of the game, let the user know how many letters the secretWord contains. * Ask the user to supply one guess (i.e. letter) per round. * The user should receive feedback immediately after each guess about whether their guess appears in the computers word. * After each round, you should also display to the user the partially guessed word so far, as well as letters that the user has not yet guessed. Follows the other limitations detailed in the problem write-up. &#39;&#39;&#39; # FILL IN YOUR CODE HERE... &lt;/textarea&gt;&lt;span class=&#34;cm-editor-exit-message capa-message&#34; id=&#34;cm-editor-exit-message-7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457_2_1&#34;&gt; Press ESC then TAB or click outside of the code editor to exit &lt;/span&gt;&lt;div class=&#34;grader-status&#34; tabindex=&#34;-1&#34;&gt;&lt;span class=&#34;status unanswered&#34; id=&#34;status_7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457_2_1&#34; data-tooltip=&#34;Not yet answered.&#34;&gt;&lt;span class=&#34;sr&#34;&gt;unanswered&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&#34;status-icon&#34; aria-hidden=&#34;true&#34;/&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p class=&#34;debug&#34;&gt;unanswered&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;span id=&#34;answer_7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457_2_1&#34;/&gt;&lt;div class=&#34;external-grader-message&#34;&gt; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;b&gt;Note: &lt;/b&gt; In &#34;See Full Output&#34;, the parameter to the hangman function is a string.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt; &lt;div class=&#34;action&#34;&gt; &lt;input type=&#34;hidden&#34; name=&#34;problem_id&#34; value=&#34;Problem 4 - The Game&#34; /&gt; &lt;div class=&#34;submit-attempt-container&#34;&gt; &lt;button type=&#34;button&#34; class=&#34;submit btn-brand&#34; data-submitting=&#34;Submitting&#34; data-value=&#34;Submit&#34; data-should-enable-submit-button=&#34;True&#34; aria-describedby=&#34;submission_feedback_7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457&#34; &gt; &lt;span class=&#34;submit-label&#34;&gt;Submit&lt;/span&gt; &lt;/button&gt; &lt;div class=&#34;submission-feedback&#34; id=&#34;submission_feedback_7c51fa66a54c4b019c4dd0f172425457&#34;&gt; You have used 0 of 30 attempts &lt;span class=&#34;sr&#34;&gt;Some problems have options such as save, reset, hints, or show answer. Problem 4

Problem 4 - The Game

0/15 points (graded)

Now you will implement the function hangman, which takes one parameter - the secretWord the user is to guess. This starts up an interactive game of Hangman between the user and the computer. Be sure you take advantage of the three helper functions, isWordGuessed, getGuessedWord, and getAvailableLetters, that you've defined in the previous part.

Hints:

  • You should start by noticing where we're using the provided functions (at the top of ps3_hangman.py) to load the words and pick a random one. Note that the functions loadWords and chooseWord should only be used on your local machine, not in the tutor. When you enter in your solution in the tutor, you only need to give your hangman function.

  • Consider using lower() to convert user input to lower case. For example:

    guess = 'A'
guessInLowerCase = guess.lower()

  • Consider writing additional helper functions if you need them!

  • There are four important pieces of information you may wish to store:

    1. secretWord: The word to guess.
    2. lettersGuessed: The letters that have been guessed so far.
    3. mistakesMade: The number of incorrect guesses made so far.
    4. availableLetters: The letters that may still be guessed. Every time a player guesses a letter, the guessed letter must be removed from availableLetters (and if they guess a letter that is not in availableLetters, you should print a message telling them they've already guessed that - so try again!).

Sample Output

The output of a winning game should look like this...
	Loading word list from file...
	55900 words loaded.
	Welcome to the game, Hangman!
	I am thinking of a word that is 4 letters long.
	-------------
	You have 8 guesses left.
	Available letters: abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz
	Please guess a letter: a
	Good guess: _ a_ _
	------------

	Available letters: bcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz
	Please guess a letter: a
	Oops! You've already guessed that letter: _ a_ _
	------------

	Available letters: bcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz
	Please guess a letter: s
	Oops! That letter is not in my word: _ a_ _

	Please guess a letter: t
	Good guess: ta_ t
	------------

	Please guess a letter: r
	Oops! That letter is not in my word: ta_ t
	------------
	You have 6 guesses left.
	Available letters: bcdefghijklmnopquvwxyz
	Please guess a letter: m
	Oops! That letter is not in my word: ta_ t
	------------
	You have 5 guesses left.
	Available letters: bcdefghijklnopquvwxyz
	Please guess a letter: c
	Good guess: tact
	------------
	Congratulations, you won!
And the output of a losing game should look like this...

Note that if you choose to use the helper functions isWordGuessed, getGuessedWord, or getAvailableLetters, you do not need to paste your definitions in the box. We have supplied our implementations of these functions for your use in this part of the problem. If you use additional helper functions, you will need to paste those definitions here.

Your function should include calls to input to get the user's guess.

Why does my Output Have None at Various Places?

None is a keyword and it comes from the fact that you are printing the result of a function that does not return anything. For example: 

    def foo(x):
        print(x)
If you just call the function with foo(3), you will see output: 
    3   #-- because the function printed the variable
However, if you do print(foo(3)), you will see output: 
    3     #-- because the function printed the variable
    None  #-- because you printed the function (and hence the return)
All functions return something. If a function you write does not return anything (and just prints something to the console), then the default action in Python is to return None
